Maigen Road Dispute Heard Yesterday 126

The Central People's Movement Committee and the Ministry of Railways Send Personnel to Persuade

Foreman Declares Abandonment of Election and Being Elected Rights

After the loading and unloading workers at Maigen Road Freight Station refused to register because the authorities deprived the four foremen of their right to be elected, the Central People's Movement Guidance Committee and the Ministry of Railways specially sent personnel to Shanghai to try to persuade them. The old foremen Shen Yuqing and others published a letter to the workers, declaring that they would abandon their right to elect and be elected. The details are as follows:

Send Personnel to Persuade 127

All the loading and unloading workers at Maigen Station were working as usual yesterday morning, refusing to register, and the order was quite good. Li Renzhu, a member of the Central People's Movement Guidance Committee, and Guo Zhongxing and Yang Ge, commissioners of the Ministry of Railways, came to Shanghai the day before yesterday to guide the establishment of the Maigen Road loading and unloading workers' office. Now, because the workers refused to register, they took on the task of persuasion and stated that 1. The election problem will be reported to the central government for instructions; 2. The temporary rules for the loading and unloading workers' office can be accepted in principle; 3. All loading and unloading workers must first register and wait for a solution.

Attitudes of Both Sides 128

According to the person in charge of the Two Roads Administration, the loading and unloading workers at Maigen Station refused to register this time due to a misunderstanding. The bureau's handling of the registration of the station and the restriction of the election rights of the four general foremen are all in accordance with the orders of the central government. Representatives of the Central People's Movement Guidance Committee and the Ministry of Railways have explained this to the workers, and this matter will be resolved soon. According to the loading and unloading workers, the former general foremen of the cooperative, Shen Yuqing and others, are extremely fair in their work and can be called models for the workers. Now that the railway bureau has exploited their right to elect and be elected, although the four general foremen have made sacrifices for the public and announced that they have abandoned their inherent rights, the workers cannot bear to sit idly by and watch them sacrifice, so they decided to fight for the restoration of their right to elect. As for the central government's order to reorganize the cooperative into an office, the temporary rules really need to be revised, and so on.

Abandon the Election 129

The former general foremen of the cooperative, Shen Yuqing and others, in order to absolutely obey the central government's and the Ministry of Railways' resolution methods, wrote a letter to all the loading and unloading workers at Maigen Station, stating: "The loading and unloading workers at the Maigen Road Station of the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway previously caused a major dispute due to the railway bureau sending Yang Minzhen to contract the work and canceling the original cooperative. Thanks to the support and supervision of the superior leaders and various groups, we were fortunate not to fail. In addition to being deeply grateful for the kindness of all parties, Yongxing and others are also very fortunate. However, after investigation by the Central Party Department and the Ministry of Railways, this case cannot be directly resolved by our cooperative and the railway bureau, so we should wait for processing. During this process, Yongxing and others only knew to supervise the workers to strictly abide by discipline and work hard, waiting for the superior to clearly judge right and wrong and protect the workers' livelihoods. This heart and this aspiration can be sworn to heaven and earth. Now, fortunately, the Central Party Department and the Ministry of Railways have discussed a solution and sent personnel to Shanghai to seek a solution. The solution is roughly divided into four points: 1. The contractor sent by the railway bureau will be resolutely cancelled; 2. The old cooperative should be reorganized into an office; 3. The office will elect two other general foremen to preside over everything; 4. The original four foremen must not be elected as foremen after the reorganization. We believe that this method is the best. Yongxing and others are very grateful to hear the news. Only this time, unfortunately, Shuixing and others have to fight for the 769 people's livelihoods with the railway bureau. Now, fortunately, the central government and the Ministry of Railways have a solution, which can still preserve the livelihoods and interests of all workers. We are very happy. We have heard that the workers and comrades still cannot let go of the fact that Yongxing and others were innocently deprived of their right to be elected and the question of the departure and retention of Yongxing and others. This is what Yongxing and others think is impossible. Although the comrades are acting out of the sincerity of loving us, we must know that loving us will hinder the path to resolving the dispute. Those who are not virtuous may even use the fact that Yongxing and others are clinging to power and deliberately instigating, so the comrades' love for us is enough to harm us. Moreover, Yongxing and others are already exhausted in this case. We originally hoped for an early and satisfactory solution to unload our burdens and to slightly reduce the suspicions of the railway bureau. This would be beneficial to both the public and the private. Yongxing and others only seek to benefit all workers, and we do not care about any personal sacrifice. Therefore, we hope that all comrades will still follow the orders in good faith, resolve the matter as soon as possible, and realize the reorganization so that all workers can work with peace of mind. We hereby declare our original intentions to dispel future misunderstandings. Yongxing and others have decided to give up their right to elect and be elected when the general foremen are re-elected in order to elect other capable people to seek permanent happiness for all workers. Please do not cling to your own opinions and have disputes, and do not re-elect the old four people to aggravate the guilt of Yongxing and others. We will be very grateful. We hereby declare, Shen Yuqing, Zheng Yongxing, Zhang Yuchang, Song Kaigui, together."

Jiangnan Shipyard Completes Assembly of British New Warship 130

Yesterday Went to Wusong Waters for Gun Testing

The Commander of the British Navy Fleet in China, after approval by the British Admiralty, ordered the construction of a new type of shallow-water warship, named the HMS Sandpiper, which was assembled by the Jiangnan Shipyard. It is scheduled to be handed over to the British Admiralty's representative for acceptance on the 20th of this month.

Construction Process 131

The design of the ship is the latest type of 1933 drawn by the British Admiralty. The various parts of the hull were assembled in England in hundreds of boxes and shipped to Shanghai in April. The Jiangnan Shipyard was entrusted to assemble them. The British Admiralty sent Lieutenant Colonel Zobt and Lieutenant Colonel Reed to Shanghai to supervise the construction. The shipyard also assigned Mr. Zheng Zhaoling, a quality inspector with shipbuilding experience, as the construction supervisor. After the start of construction, a launching ceremony was held in June. Mrs. Mao Gen, the chief engineer of the shipyard, broke the bottle. It has now been completed.

Gun Testing Yesterday 132

After the completion of the various parts of the project, in addition to going to Longhua four times to test the engine, it sailed to the waters outside the Wusongkou for the first gun test at 6:00 AM yesterday morning. A total of 28 shells were fired from the front and rear guns. The firing force was very sufficient, with each shell reaching a range of 10 miles, about 30 Chinese miles. It did not return to Shanghai until about 5:00 PM. In addition, the engine test results showed a speed of more than 12 knots per hour.

Assignment of Captain 133

After the completion of the ship, the full list of officers for the entire vessel, as learned by the Huadong News Agency reporter, includes Commander Ash, Lieutenant Commander Gullot, Inspectors Mr. Reed and Lieutenant Colonels Hclt, Chief Engineer Guelon, and Second Engineer Cor, all of whom are British naval officers stationed in China and familiar with the situation in China.

Overall Ship Structure 134

The total tonnage of the ship is 167 tons, with 30 tons for the machinery and 115 tons for the hull. It is 210 feet long, 30 feet wide, and has a draft of 2 feet. Its speed is 12 nautical miles per hour. It has two cannons, both of which are the latest models from 1933. The front cannon is named the Six-Pound Cannon, and the rear cannon is named the 3.7-inch Cannon. The bottom is black, and the hull is light gray.

Transfer and Flag Raising 135

According to Mr. Zheng Zhangling, the ship's inspector, speaking to the Huadong News Agency reporter, the ship began construction on April 3rd and is now complete. The engineering aspect was exceptionally rapid. The British side was quite cautious about this project, and in addition to sending me to supervise, they also sent engineer Wang Rong, electrician Gong Zhenfeng, and construction worker Sun Jingyang to work together. The British side highly praised this rapid project. It has now been decided to transfer the ship to British naval personnel stationed in Shanghai on the 20th of this month for acceptance. Furthermore, it is determined that the ship will raise its flag and join the fleet on September 1st.

Wolf Mountain Cannon Test 136

Additionally, the national cruiser H.M.S. Montis plans to test fire machine guns near the Wolf Mountain river area on the 22nd of this month. The ship will also test fire cannons at the mouth of the Yangtze River on the 23rd of the same month, and the British Consul General in Shanghai, Mr. Davison, has prepared a document to notify the Municipal Government to avoid misunderstandings among various land and sea military and police agencies. It is now learned that the Municipal Government has informed the Municipal Public Security Bureau, the Security Division, and the First Fleet Headquarters of the Navy.

Reply from the Tax Bureau to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

On the Expression of Fixed-Amount Tax on Local Wine 140

New taxes should be assessed and collected in accordance with regulations

Strikes and cessation of brewing are inappropriate

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously received letters from local yellow wine guilds, stating that after the promulgation of the fixed-amount tax, the printing certificates were canceled, and the industry was on the verge of extinction. The general meeting of all members resolved to strike and cease transportation and requested to forward the matter to the Tax Bureau for revision. The Tax Bureau immediately sent a letter to the Ministry of Finance's Taxation Department. The reply from the department, which is transcribed below, is sent directly: Letter No. 482 from your council has been received. The special printing certificate is an evil practice left over from the Beijing lower government era. This revision of the tax system eliminates long-standing abuses and unifies collection. There is no reason to retain the printing certificate. The fixed-amount tax on local goods should be assessed and collected in accordance with regulations. The collecting agency cannot make extra demands, and merchants must not seek to pay less. The guild directly presented a petition earlier, which was refuted in detail by the ministry. The refutation is copied and sent for reference. As for the guild's original letter stating that the new tax hinders business, how it hinders business is not stated, and there is no way to verify it. In short, for the sake of reorganizing tax revenue, the new regulations are imperative. Regarding the difficulties that merchants believe exist in the procedures, all those that do not violate principles have been ordered by the department to be changed as appropriate to understand the merchants' situation. The guild should not insist on its own opinions, regardless of the right and wrong of the matter, and use the cessation of transportation and brewing as unreasonable demands to disrupt the reorganization of the tax system, which is inappropriate. As for freedom of business, it should not be interfered with by others. The guild even declared in a circular to all workers in the workshops to stop working and sent many people to monitor the sections. If this is implemented, it is close to hindering the same industry and obstructing tax administration. It should be known that this kind of action has exceeded the scope stipulated by the Public Association Law and should be corrected immediately. If the guild continues to make trouble unreasonably, the department will only handle it in accordance with the law and will not be lenient. Your council leads the merchants and understands the general situation. Please inform all the merchants accordingly.

Founding Record of Sheng Sheng Midwifery School 145

Gathering the Great Qi of the Medical Community

Striving for Popularization

Midwifery in our country has always been handled by uneducated midwives, resulting in countless lives lost. Now, Shanghai medical professionals Yu Yunxiu, Wang Qizhang, Xu Jihua, Wang Yugang, Zhu Qiluo, Liu Wushu, Xia Shenchu, Cai Yumen, Jiang Zhenxun, Ye Hancheng, Xu Xiangsun and others, after consulting with obstetric specialist Dr. Qu Shaoheng, founded the Sheng Sheng Midwifery School, aiming to cultivate specialized midwifery talent and teach the essentials of various medical subjects to improve and develop obstetrics and strive for popularization. The school board has been approved by the Municipal Education Bureau and will start enrollment immediately. Any woman aged 18 to 35 with a junior high school diploma or equivalent qualifications can apply. Kunshan Road is Packed with People

Watching the Arrest of the Murderer in the Cased Corpse Case 146

=The Portuguese Consul Only Signed the Arrest Warrant Yesterday Afternoon After the Police Station Presented Evidence=

=The Murderer's Brothers Were Arrested at the Same Time; the Family Members Did Not Seem Alarmed at All=

│Currently Temporarily Detained in the West Prison on Xiamen Road; the Portuguese Consul is Scheduled to Hold a Preliminary Hearing This Morning│

The sensational cased corpse case, after several changes, was not until the 12th that the chief of the Japanese consulate police, Hanari, worked hard to investigate and found the principal offender. Because the Portuguese consul delayed the issuance of the arrest warrant until noon yesterday, the murderer and his accomplice, who moved the corpse to Japan, were arrested under the heavy encirclement of the police station and the Japanese consulate police. The two murderers have been sent to the West Prison on Xiamen Road to await interrogation. The details of the arrest yesterday are recorded as follows:

It Took One Week from Discovery to Solving the Case 147

The cased corpse case discovered in the Shanghai Maru ship occurred on the 7th of this month, and Shanghai's investigation also began on that day. Initially, it was difficult to find clues, and the Russian was initially suspected. Then, Chen Qiaoying was mistakenly identified. It was not until the 10th that Chen Qiaoying went to the Japanese consulate to prove that it was untrue. The chief of the Japanese police station, Hanari, and the police chiefs Aika and Sato, spent more than twenty hours investigating, and as a result, the location of the principal offender and the details of the tragic murder were found. Then they surrounded the location to prevent the criminal from escaping. The speed of solving the case was truly astonishing. However, due to the relationship of extraterritoriality, foreigners could not be immediately arrested for committing crimes in the concession. An arrest warrant must be requested from the consul of their country of residence before they can be arrested. Portuguese Consul Xue Erfo delayed the arrest warrant requested by the police station for this arrest from the 11th until noon yesterday. It took exactly one week from the discovery of the case to the capture of the principal offender.

The Portuguese Consul Signed the Arrest Warrant at Noon Yesterday 148

Since the morning of the 11th, the Japanese consulate sent police detectives to surround the house where the murderer lived at No. C-174, Yifeng Lane, Kunshan Road. Hanari immediately reported to the Japanese Consul and transferred the case to the Public Concession Police Station for handling. On Saturday, the Board of Works, based on the report of the chief of the Japanese police station, also presented strong evidence and negotiated with Portuguese Consul Xue Erfo stationed in Shanghai to request the issuance of an arrest warrant for the arrest of the murderer, Bade Lie Limidio. Because the time was late that day, there was no reply. The next day was a Sunday rest and office closed, so the arrest warrant was delayed. Until yesterday morning, after the Board of Works urged, Portuguese Consul Xue Erfo finally issued the arrest warrant at 12:30 in the morning and handed it over to the police station for execution.

A Large Force of Police Arrests the Murderer 149

After the police station obtained the arrest warrant, it dispatched a large number of detectives around 2:00 PM, led by Western Detective Chief Weishi with more than 20 people, first to the Japanese consulate to meet with the chief of the Japanese police station, Hanari, and Japanese police officers, and went to No. C-174, Yifeng Lane, Kunshan Road. At that time, the house was still surrounded by Japanese police. At that time, there were three arrest warrants: one for the arrest of the principal offender, one for the arrest of the accomplice's brother, and another for permission to enter the house for search. When Western Detective Chief William Earth led the Chinese and Western detectives into No. C-174, Yifeng Lane, the custodial police of the criminal section of the Japanese consulate released the detectives into the house. The idlers watching there were crowded, with as many as two to three thousand people, blocking traffic. Chinese and Western detectives maintained temporary order and closed the iron gate of Yifeng Lane, driving away the idlers. No. C-174 is in the fifth alley of Yifeng Lane. After the Chinese and Western detectives entered the house, they showed the Portuguese Consul's arrest warrant and arrested both the principal offender, Bade Lie Limidio, and the accomplice, the brother of the principal offender, Qiu Sha Fu Limidio.

Sent to the West Prison on Xiamen Road for Temporary Custody 150

When Western Detective Chief Williams of the police station entered the house and showed the arrest warrant signed by the Portuguese Consul, the principal offender, Bade Lie Limidio, and the accomplice, the brother of the principal offender, Qiu Sha Fu Limidio, did not resist and were willing to go to the police station with the Chinese and Western detectives. At the time of the arrest, the family members of the offenders did not show any panic and were calm. Western Detective Chief Williams took the two murderers to Yifeng Lane and had them escorted to the car by the detectives. It was heard that because the Portuguese consulate had no place for detention, they were sent to the West Prison on Xiamen Road for temporary custody to await interrogation. The murderers were arrested and taken out of the lane at 3:00 PM. The custodial police of the criminal section of the Japanese consulate, who were sent to surround the house to guard the offenders, also withdrew after the murderers were arrested.

The Portuguese Consulate Issued a Statement Yesterday on the Issuance of the Warrant 151

Regarding the delay in issuing the arrest warrant, the Portuguese Consulate issued a statement yesterday by Mr. Laijie, who signed the warrant, stating that after receiving the notification from the Public Concession Police Station on Saturday, the consulate immediately prepared to issue the arrest warrant. The reason why it was not signed immediately was that the consulate was waiting for the police station to present sufficient evidence. The consulate for arresting the murderer (in black) in the cased corpse case (photographed by Gong Shuxian) should immediately arrest any Portuguese citizen in Shanghai if they commit a crime and will never protect them. Recently, newspapers have reported that the Portuguese consulate deliberately made things difficult, etc. In fact, the reason why the arrest warrant was delayed was not the consulate, but the police station's time-consuming investigation. Now the case has been returned to the Portuguese consulate for interrogation, but because Portugal has no prison in Shanghai and no establishment of the Ancha Envoy Department, it is temporarily kept in the West Prison on Xiamen Road to await the Portuguese consulate's interrogation at any time. It is learned that the Portuguese consulate will interrogate the offender at the consulate at 11:00 AM this morning.

The Murderer's Bad Conduct is Scorned by the Neighbors 152

The principal offender, Bade Lie Limidio, and the accomplice, are both of extremely poor character. According to the gatekeeper of Yifeng Lane, the two brothers often committed crimes against vendors in the lane. Not long ago, they beat a vendor in the lane. They had been to the police station, and the case had not yet been closed. In addition, they owed a lot of goods in various stores, and there were often people who came to the door to ask for them and were insulted by the two. Therefore, people in the neighborhood despise the behavior of these two.

Mr. Lin took the Japanese ship Nagasaki Maru, which was scheduled to arrive in Shanghai at 3:00 PM yesterday. The Japanese consulate in Shanghai has received a telegram. Four Robbers Hijack a Car 154

=But No Case Has Occurred in This City=

=The Empty Car Was Found on the Bund of Sima Road=

Yesterday morning, a taxi rented from the Far East Automobile Company at No. 1 Pingliang Road, Yangshupu, was hijacked on Jungong Road. The empty car was found in the afternoon. After a thorough investigation by the city's police agencies, no case was found. The details are described below:

Four Customers Rent a Car 155

The Far East Automobile Company is located at No. 1 Pingliang Road, Yangpu. At around 8:25 AM yesterday morning, four customers suddenly came to the company. One was wearing a black Xiangyunsha short shirt and pants, and one was wearing a brown suit and white drill pants. They both spoke with Jiangbei accents. There were also two people, one wearing a blue striped silk shirt and pants, and one wearing a blue cloth shirt and pants. They looked like Chinese, but their language was stiff and similar to Japanese. At that time, the person wearing Xiangyunsha went to the company's accounting room and said that he wanted to rent a car to the Yangshupu Electric Light Factory and paid one yuan. The company assigned driver Wu Chunshan, a Ningbo native, to drive a concession license No. 17718 and a city license No. 4370 car out. The four people got into the car one after another and went east.

Hijacking the Car Midway 156

Unexpectedly, the four people in the car suddenly changed their destination midway,

Ordering the driver to turn to Jungong Road, Yinxiang Port. Driver Wu Chunshan immediately turned to Jungong Road as ordered. When the car was about to drive to the intersection of Jungong Road and Chunjiang Road, one of the four people in the back suddenly used a hemp rope to put around Wu's throat and pulled hard. At the same time, the person wearing the suit took out a pistol and threatened Wu, forbidding him to make a sound. At this time, Wu Chunshan knew that something was wrong and quickly slammed on the brakes. However, another person next to him stuffed a towel into the driver's mouth and dragged him out of the car, tied his hands and feet with a rope, and pushed him aside. They got back into the car and drove it themselves to the concession. Seeing that the car had gone far away, Wu Chunshan struggled hard and managed to break free after a long time. He took the towel out of his mouth and ran to the nearby Fourth Precinct of the Fifth District to report.

Empty Car Found 157

After receiving the report, the precinct immediately dispatched a large number of police officers to search everywhere, but because the time was too late, they found nothing. They immediately returned to the precinct to report. At the same time, driver Wu Chunshan also called the company to report the incident. Therefore, the company immediately reported to Huishan and other police stations, requesting investigation. The Fourth Precinct of the Fifth District also urgently sent telegrams to the General Bureau and various districts, the French Concession, etc., requesting assistance in the search. For a time, detectives were everywhere, and the situation was serious. There were no clues until noon. Unexpectedly, around 4:00 PM, the car was suddenly found near the Bund of Sima Road. After the guard spotted it, he quickly returned to the Central Police Station to report. The police station dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to investigate and found that only an empty car was parked there. They inspected the footprints and handprints in the car, and there was no hurried or chaotic state. They tried to print the fingerprints and footprints left in the car and brought them back to the police station for filing in order to investigate. They also notified the Far East Automobile Company to send a driver to drive the car back around 5:00 PM. However, since the four people hijacked the car, they must have had some intention, but now there is no follow-up, which is very confusing. The Ministry of Industry is Merging

Shanghai-Qingdao Serum Manufacturing Plant 158

=Expand the Scope of Organization; the Plant Site is Still Under Investigation in Shanghai=

=Prepare a Fund of 50 Million Upon Minister Song's Return to the Country to Handle=

Recently, the Ministry of Industry has stated that the domestically produced serum cannot meet the needs of the entire country, resulting in reliance on foreign countries. The number of leaks per year is more than one million. Therefore, it has ordered the Qingdao and Shanghai serum manufacturing plants to proceed with the merger to form a large-scale serum manufacturing plant. The plant site will still be built in Shanghai. As soon as Finance Minister Song returns to the country, a meeting will be held to raise funds to handle it. The news obtained by the Huadong News Agency is recorded as follows:

Merger of Two Places 159

In recent years, animal diseases have been prevalent, and the demand for serum is very high. The Ministry of Industry previously sent letters to Qingdao and Shanghai, each of which has a serum manufacturing plant. However, because the scale is too small and the equipment is lacking, the serum produced is very small. In total, the output of the two manufacturing plants is not enough for the summer season. Now, in order to recover rights and interests and increase serum production, it has been decided to merge the Qingdao and Shanghai plants to form a large-scale serum manufacturing plant.

Sending Personnel to the United States 160

Regarding the various machines for manufacturing serum, it has been decided to first raise 500,000 yuan to send personnel to the United States to purchase them. This is because the existing machines at the Qingdao and Shanghai manufacturing plants are not only extremely weak in manufacturing capacity, but also mostly no longer applicable. However, this funding matter must await Mr. Song's return to the country before a collective discussion and allocation can be made. At the same time, it will also be decided to hire foreign technicians to improve product quality.

Plant Site Established in Shanghai 161

As for the plant site issue, it has been decided to establish it in Shanghai. The Ministry of Industry will send personnel to Shanghai within days to inspect the site in order to commence construction and proceed with the merger. After this serum plant is officially established, its output quantity must at least be able to supply the entire country's needs, so that it no longer relies on foreign countries. It is estimated that more than a million yuan of foreign outflow can be recovered annually.

Personnel and Administration 162

In addition, all personnel and administrative matters of the plant after its establishment will remain under the direct jurisdiction of the Ministry of Industry. The position of plant director will be taken over by the director of the Shanghai plant, with the director of the Qingdao plant as his deputy. In addition to the existing personnel from both plants, due to the expanded scale, it is planned to request the transfer of several experienced and knowledgeable officials from the National Health Administration to work at the plant.

Page 16

Apprentice Starts Fire in the Middle of the Night 163

=Detected by Companion, Prevents Major Disaster=

=Intended to Escape, Resorting to This Last Resort=

│Sentenced to Two Years Imprisonment, Suspended for Five Years│

Zhu Fu'an from Ningbo, only seventeen years old, was an apprentice at the Hexing Machinery Factory at 784 Gongping Road. He has been working at the store for only two months to date. At 1:30 AM on the 13th, while everyone was sound asleep, Fu'an suddenly soaked newspapers in kerosene and placed them in the factory's firewood pile, intending to start a fire. When thick smoke filled the air and flames blazed, fortunately another apprentice in the factory, Xin Xianzhong, woke up and immediately roused everyone. He also reported to the fire brigade. By the time the fire truck arrived, the fire had been extinguished. The incident was reported to the local police station, who took the owner of the factory, Liu Zhixiang, and the apprentices and workers to the police station for questioning. As a result of the investigation, it was discovered that Zhu Fu'an had committed the above-mentioned act, a crime under Article 187 of the Criminal Law. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Special District Court, where Judge Wu Zehan presided over the trial in the Third Criminal Court. First, the police lawyer reported the above situation, and stated that the police investigation into the reason for Zhu Fu'an's arson revealed that he did not want to work at the factory. However, this reason was not reasonable. He had only been at the factory for two months and wanted to leave. Moreover, even if his wish to leave was granted, he would inevitably be punished by his parents. Therefore, he was still reluctantly working at the factory. However, the factory's mistress, Liu Liu, 20 years old, had a good relationship with the apprentice and treated him very well. All the money for shopping in the store was entrusted to him for safekeeping. Recently, she entrusted him with 25 yuan to purchase items at any time. Later, the factory owner Liu Zhixiang found out that only half of what he had reported had been spent. He severely reprimanded Liu Liu and sent her back to her parents' home. Zhu Fu'an was also reprimanded. The mistress's preferential treatment was also a major reason why Zhu did not immediately leave the factory. Now that the person who treated him well was forced to separate, and he himself had long wanted to leave, he set fire to the store. When questioned, Zhu Fu'an admitted without hesitation. Liu Zhixiang also went to court to testify to everything, and said that the apprentice was young and ignorant. In addition to sending a telegram to his father in Shanghai to take him back and discipline him, he requested the court to be lenient and not impose a heavy sentence. The pro bono lawyer Yan Yinshi rose to defend him. The court sentenced him to two years' imprisonment, suspended for five years, and Judge Wu explained the reasons for the judgment, saying that the defendant's arson only charred the nearby door, and fortunately did not cause a major disaster, so it was treated as an attempted crime. He was still young and his actions were inexcusable. It was hoped that he would repent and start anew, so he was granted a suspended sentence. If he commits another crime during the probation period, it will be executed together.

=Large Number of Opium Pipes Seized=

=Arrested Offenders to Be Punished Separately=

Chief Detective Lu Dagong of the General Police Station learned that someone had privately established an opium den inside No. 258 Jiyi Lane, Nanjing Road, for people to smoke opium. He then reported to the First Special Court and signed a search warrant. At 10:00 AM the day before yesterday, he went to the address with Chief Detective Xing Ziquan of the Chinese police. First, he cracked down on the opium den in the east rear厢房 downstairs, and arrested the owner Chen Baoxiang and four customers, Wang Bingquan, Qian Zongli, Zhang Bingkun, etc. He confiscated 30 gambling books, 77 small boxes of opium, hundreds of empty opium boxes, and many opium pipes and lamps. Then, in the front east厢房, which was a Dingxin Foreign Goods store, he confiscated an opium pipe, an opium lamp, and a jar of opium, and arrested two people, Huang Xiaoquan and Xie Baozhen. In the west廂房 upstairs, which was the Guan Jianji Cloth Store, he confiscated a jar of opium, and arrested one person, Zhu Menggeng. In the west廂房 downstairs, the Fu Cheng Cloth Store, he confiscated a piece of raw opium weighing 31 and a half taels, an opium pipe, and two opium holders, and arrested four people, Song Xianglin, Zhu Ganzhang, Wang Shouming, and Ye Rensheng. All of them were taken back to the police station. Except for Zhu Menggeng, Song Xianglin, Zhu Ganzhang, Wang Shouming, and Ye Rensheng, who were each allowed to be released on bail for 260 yuan, the rest were detained. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Criminal Division of the First Special Court, and the police lawyer Ru Bao Yi explained the case and prosecuted them separately in accordance with Articles 10, 11, and 13 of the Opium Suppression Law. Wang Bingquan and Qian Zongli each hired lawyers Fan Gang and Wu Linkun to defend them. When questioned, Chen Baoxiang denied that the opium den was established by him, and said that it was established by Zhang Bingkun. After a detailed investigation by the court and questioning of the defendants, Court Director Feng Shide then announced the verdict in court, sentencing Zhang Bingkun to one year of imprisonment and a fine of 60 yuan, Chen Baoxiang to two months of imprisonment, Song Xianglin and Zhu Ganzhang each to a fine of 60 yuan, Wang Bingquan, Qian Zongli, and Guan Jianji (i.e. Zhu Menggeng) each to a fine of 30 yuan, Huang Xiaoquan and Xie Baozhen each to a fine of 20 yuan. The opium tools and other items were all confiscated. Wang Shouming and Ye Rensheng were found not guilty.

Revision of Special Price Measures for Cotton Yarn on Two Railways 173

Beneficial to Both Railway and Commercial Parties

The Ministry of Railways Approves Trial Implementation for One Year

The Ministry of Railways has learned that the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways have been transporting cotton yarn and cotton cloth. In the past, due to water transport competition, special prices were set to attract business. It is now found that the special price for this project was originally reported by the merchants for transport, and expired at the end of May this year. However, the special price for this project has been in place for a long time, and it is not applicable. Moreover, the price does not distinguish between high-quality and ordinary cotton yarn, and the freight is charged at 45% less than the third-class less-than-carload freight rate. The freight for精製cotton yarn and cloth is charged at 70% less than the second-class less-than-carload freight rate, and ordinary cotton yarn and cloth are charged at 45% less than the fourth-class less-than-carload freight rate. For example, the freight from Shanghai to Beijing is 1角 per 50 kg for精製and ordinary. This seems to be too much pressure on domestic goods cloth. Therefore, the existence of this special price not only benefits idlers, but also affects the future development of Chinese yarn and cloth. It is really not

The way to promote domestic goods. The ministry has seen this

So it ordered to revise the special price. Recently, the two railway bureaus have submitted a report to the Ministry of Railways for review and abolition of the special price for cotton yarn and cotton cloth, and a revised special price for cotton yarn.

This seems to be beneficial to both the railway and commercial parties. However, the ministry has approved a one-year trial period to observe the effectiveness. The revised special price measures are recorded as follows: 1. High-quality cotton yarn will be reduced by 20% from the third-class freight rate. If the shipper has a certificate from the National Cotton Yarn Industry Association when reporting to the station, it will be reduced by another 20%. For example, the freight for cotton yarn from Shanghai to Beijing without a certificate is 2角 per 50 kg, and the freight for cotton yarn with a certificate is 1角6分. 2. Ordinary cotton yarn will be reduced by 20% from the fourth-class freight rate. If the shipper has a certificate from the National Cotton Yarn Industry Association when reporting to the station, it will be reduced by another 20%. For example, the freight for cotton yarn from Shanghai to Beijing without a certificate is 1角4分 per 50 kg, and the freight for cotton yarn with a certificate is 1角1分. 3. 精製cotton yarn and cloth will be reduced by 20% from the second-class freight rate. If the shipper has a certificate from the National Cotton Yarn Industry Association when reporting to the station, it will be reduced by another 20%. For example, the freight for cotton yarn and cloth from Shanghai to Beijing without a certificate is 2角9分 per 50 kg, and the freight for cotton yarn and cloth with a certificate is 2角3分. 4. Ordinary cotton yarn and cloth will be reduced by 20% from the fourth-class freight rate. If the shipper has a certificate from the National Cotton Yarn Industry Association when reporting to the station, it will be reduced by another 20%. For example, the freight for cotton yarn and cloth from Shanghai to Beijing without a certificate is 1角4分 per 50 kg, and the freight for cotton yarn and cloth with a certificate is 1角1分.

Banning the Giving of Coupons for Cigarette Gifts 175

Tax Administration Letter to Cigarette Factory Association

The Ministry of Finance Tax Administration has recently seen that cigarette gifts have become increasingly popular. It specially approved the Da Yun Company's request and forwarded a letter to the Shanghai Chinese Cigarette Factory Industry Association, notifying all member cigarette factories to stop giving gifts as soon as possible. The letter is recorded as follows: Respectfully, the case according to the repeated approvals of the National Government Aviation Highway Construction Lottery Ticket Office, the method of banning cash gifts from cigarette companies has been communicated to your association to cancel immediately, and to correct the method and order the Tongshui Bureau in the Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui regions to forward the order to the resident factory staff to pay attention to the case. Later, according to a letter from Huadong Company, requesting that the awarding of betel nut cigarettes and empty shells be allowed to end within a limited time, and then the cash would be cancelled and replaced with goods when the lottery tickets were issued next time. After reporting the situation to the Aviation Lottery Ticket Office for review and reply, the reply stated that the company's gift giving was about to expire and it was reasonable to maintain credibility. However, the original letter did not recognize that the company's handling of this lottery ticket promotion affected the promotion of the construction lottery tickets. On the contrary, the original letter stated that the Ministry had prejudices against the company, which was not in the national interest and ignorant of the matter. Now that your department has approved the consultation in the letter, the office can agree to the lenient handling of this matter. The other companies with a long time to give gifts should still be ordered to stop or revise the method first. As for the method of competing for sales when cigarette companies discuss and move sales channels in the future, please also order in advance that the following principles should be strictly observed: 1. No tickets of any kind shall be printed and issued. 2. Cash shall not be used as gifts. 3. The tops of gifts shall not be awarded based on the numbers of formally issued lottery tickets and other tickets. Correspondently, I would like to inform your department for investigation and hope that you will quickly forward the order to all cigarette companies to comply. At the same time, I would like to order the Tongshui Bureau of the Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui regions to forward the order to the resident factory staff to pay close attention at all times and seriously correct the matter. Aside from directly informing Huadong Company to comply and ordering the Tongshui Bureau of the Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui regions to inform the resident factory staff, I am writing to your association to inform you for investigation and hope that you will quickly forward the order to all cigarette companies to comply with the matter.

Strict Inspection After the Arrival of the Taiyuan Steamer in Shanghai

Due to Rumors of Dapeng Bay Pirates Coming to Shanghai

The Zilin News reported that since the local area received a telegram from Hong Kong about the news of 13 Dapeng Bay pirates coming to Shanghai, at 5:30 PM yesterday (13), the Taigu Company's Taiyuan steamer arrived in Shanghai from the south. A large number of detectives from the French Concession police station, together with the customs water police station, guarded the surrounding area of the pier. After the passengers and luggage disembarked, the customs officers first, and then the police, conducted two detailed searches. It took a total of two hours, but no firearms were confiscated and no suspicious persons were seen. According to the Taiyuan shipowner, the ship departed from Hong Kong on Wednesday afternoon, arrived in Xiamen on Thursday afternoon, and set sail to Shanghai on Friday afternoon, and arrived in port on Sunday. No suspicious persons were seen along the way, and no one on the ship heard the Hong Kong police's report that pirates were going to Shanghai. According to Hong Kong news, the Hong Kong police had cracked down on 13 pirates and found several pistols in the hidden bottom buckets they were carrying. They confessed that another 13 people had already set off to Shanghai. It is expected that other ships coming from the south will also be searched as strictly in the next day or two.

Shanghai-Minhang Long-Distance Bus

Added Special Bus to Zhapu Seaside Bathing 176

│Buses Depart Today···Three Buses Daily│

Huangshan, near Zhapu, Zhejiang, is located on the coast and has excellent scenery. It is a natural seaside bathing beach. There are many people from all over the world who admire its name and want to visit, but they all feel that transportation is inconvenient, so they cannot get what they want. It is now learned that the Shanghai-Minhang Long-Distance Bus Company has decided to launch a special bus to Zhapu for seaside bathing, starting today, in order to facilitate people from China and abroad to go to seaside bathing. The bus goes directly from Shanghai to Huangshan and departs three times a day. The price is very cheap. It is also heard that the gentry in Zhapu, in view of the fact that a Western youth was washed away by the waves and tragically drowned because he did not know the tide and the depth of the beach, have now set up striking signs to warn all swimmers to prevent future troubles.

120,000 Huge Robbery Case

The Innocent Are Released Yesterday 177

The 129,080-yuan mega-robbery case that occurred on Yong'an Street in the French Concession last month has been solved by the French police, who arrested the thieves Zhang Wei-cai, Wang Mao-nan, and Li A-long. They were sent to court for trial. The escaped thief, Da Luo-song, also known as Jiang Gai-yuan, evaded capture, fled to other cities with the stolen goods, and was wanted by the police with a reward. He has not yet been apprehended. Earlier this month, the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau's Detective Squad arrested Da Luo-song's wife, Jiang Qin-shi, and mother-in-law, Qin Zhang-shi, in Zhangjia浜, Pudong, and found 2,000 yuan of the original stolen banknotes in Zhang's home. They were taken to the bureau for interrogation. Subsequently, four men and women, including Da Luo-song's relatives Ma Yong-lian, Ma Yong-chang, Ma Wan-shi, and Da Luo-song's concubine Jiang Ma-shi, were apprehended in Taihe Street, Yangshupu Road, and sent to the First Special District Court. Jin Jiu-lin, Inspector General of the French Police Special Agency, and Deputy Detective Zhou Yao-ting, among others, went to the court and transferred Jiang Qin-shi and Qin Zhang-shi, along with the stolen banknotes and the six men and women including Ma Yong-lian, to the Second Special District Court for interrogation and investigation. Details of the case were reported earlier. At 11:30 a.m. yesterday, Judge Li Chang-nian conducted a trial in the Criminal Division of the Second Special District Court. First, the police lawyer Gu Shou-xi presented the case, stating that the police investigation had found that the first to fifth defendants, Ma Yong-lian, Ma Yong-chang, Ma Wan-shi, Jiang Ma-shi, and Jiang Qin-shi, were not related to the case. Therefore, the police would not prosecute them and requested their release. However, the sixth defendant, Qin Zhang-shi, knowingly received and concealed stolen goods from the robbery. She was charged with receiving stolen goods under Article 376 of the Criminal Code, and the court was requested to handle the case according to the law. The stolen banknotes were presented to the court. Subsequently, Wang Xing-shi, Xu Jin-qing, and Weng Lai-ke, representatives of the Wenzhou banking industry and representatives of the victim, submitted a bond issued by Wu Shao-ting, manager of the Xiaodongmen branch of the Shanghai Bank, requesting the return of the recovered stolen banknotes of 2,000 yuan. The court verified the report, briefly questioned each defendant about their name, and then ordered the five defendants, including Ma Yong-lian, to withdraw. According to Qin Zhang-shi's testimony, she was 45 years old, Da Luo-song was her son-in-law, and the banknotes were sent by Da Luo-song's brother, A-gen, to be temporarily deposited with her. He said he got them from selling forty mu of land in Shandong. The money was placed in a pottery jar in the kitchen and had not been touched. When the Public Security Bureau came to search, the money was still in the jar. She did not know where Da Luo-song was hiding. The court reviewed the testimony and, considering that Zhang-shi was an ignorant woman who did not know the origin of the banknotes and had not touched them afterwards, concluded that she could not be considered guilty. Qin Zhang-shi was acquitted and released in court. The court also ordered that Ma Yong-lian, Ma Yong-chang, Ma Wan-shi, Jiang Ma-shi, and Jiang Qin-shi should be released since the police would not prosecute them. The stolen banknotes were to be returned to the representatives of the victim.

The monk Lang Qing of Zhabei Sun Temple was falsely accused to the Public Security Bureau of privately setting up a flower fair and using counterfeit money. Medical Doctor Yu Lin Comes to Shanghai to Practice Medicine 179

Yu Lin, a current medical officer of the National Government, Director of the Chengnan Hospital in Nanjing, and Doctor of Medicine, studied in Japan for eighteen years. After graduating from the Faculty of Medicine of Kyushu Imperial University, he served as an attending physician at the university's affiliated hospital for six years. He also devoted himself to research in the classroom of Professor Goto Shichiro, a renowned surgeon, and fully grasped its essence, thereby obtaining a doctorate in medicine. His doctoral dissertation, "Blood Chemical Changes After Bacterial Toxins Enter the Blood," was published in the Japanese Surgical Society, Kyushu Medical Society, Fukuoka Medical Journal, and Japanese Journal of Medical Sciences. In 1928, he was hired by the Nanjing Municipal Gulou Hospital as the Director of Surgery. In 1930, he became a medical officer of the National Government and established the Chengnan Hospital in Nanjing, earning a remarkable reputation. Now, at the invitation of friends in Shanghai, he has come to Shanghai to set up a clinic at No. 9, Changfeng Lane, Tongfu Road, and will open on the 20th to serve patients.

The Shanghai First District Knitting Industry Workers' Union held its second members' representatives' meeting at the Xiaoximen Youth Propaganda Corps yesterday morning at 10:00 a.m. Fifty-four member representatives, including Ruan Yu-ying, attended. Letter 185

To the Editor:

Regarding the report in your newspaper on August 8 that five workers from the shipbuilding and woodworking industry, including He Qin and Qu Gen, were detained by the Municipal Party Department after petitioning for their release, it has been found that the Second Branch of the Shipbuilding and Woodworking Workers' Union has repeatedly oppressed workers, and over 200 workers were dissatisfied. They elected He Qin, Qu Gen, Mo Kuan, Su Xiang, and Huo Song as representatives to petition the Municipal Party Department for investigation. Unexpectedly, they were detained. On that day, over 140 workers gathered to petition the Municipal Party Department, demanding the release of the representatives, and the order was excellent. The Public Security Bureau did not send police to suppress them. Dai Youheng, a civil affairs officer from the Municipal Party Department, received them. Finally, Commissioner Lu Jingshi agreed to release them the next morning. The workers were satisfied and withdrew. Now that the Municipal Party Department has investigated and clarified the matter and released them, the details reported in your newspaper are inconsistent with the facts. To avoid confusion, a corresponding letter is sent, hoping that you will investigate and correct it promptly.

Respectfully,

Representatives of over 200 Cantonese workers in the shipbuilding and woodworking industry, Huo Yun.

Dated August 14, 1933, Republic of China

Address: No. 553, Dexing Lane, Peng Road

To the Editor:

I am writing to you on behalf of the abbot of the Sun Temple, Yue Jin, who stated that since the monks have resided in and managed the Sun Temple, they have been dedicated to practicing Buddhism and observing the precepts, and have never deviated from the norms. Unexpectedly, on July 28, the nearby Public Security Bureau, believing false reports from treacherous individuals, suddenly dispatched police officers to the temple and arrested the monks residing there, including Lang Qing, on suspicion of using counterfeit money and participating in gambling flower fairs. After being transferred from the district office to the Municipal Public Security Bureau, they were fortunately found to have no criminal suspicion and were released on bail a few days ago. In its reply to the Shanghai Buddhist Association, the Municipal Public Security Bureau stated, "The case has been fully investigated, and the evidence of guilt against the defendants is insufficient. In addition to complying with the instructions to release them on bail, a corresponding letter is hereby sent." This proves that after the monks were investigated and released, major local newspapers suddenly published news about the case, not only deliberately exaggerating the facts to sensationalize them, but also omitting the fact that the Municipal Public Security Bureau had investigated and determined that the defendants had no criminal suspicion and had allowed them to be released on bail. This situation clearly shows a deliberate attempt to damage the reputation of the temple. Therefore, I have been entrusted to send a letter on behalf of the lawyer to various newspapers, making a clear statement and requesting prompt correction to ensure accuracy.

Respectfully,

Lawyer Wu Zhiping

Page 17

Spring and Autumn

People 188

— Xianxian

Everyone knows that things with [round heads and square feet] are [people]. But [people] are not a simple issue and are somewhat mysterious.

If everyone with [round heads and square feet] acted as [unconditional people], the whole world would be [harmonious]. However, [people] also have racial differences.

For example, even if they have the same high noses, blue eyes, and blonde hair, they are divided into [British people] and [American people]. Even among the [people] on the European continent, there are [Germans], [French], [Westerners], and [Russians]. Moreover, even among the [Germans], there is a distinction between [old-brand Germans] and [Jews]. How strange!

Let's talk about the [people] in Asia. Indeed, they all have [round heads and square feet], but those with dark skin and clean-shaven faces are called [Filipinos], those with dark skin and pensive faces are called [Indians], those who are short and wiry are called [Japanese], and those who are large and useless are called [Koreans].

Now let's talk about the [Chinese], who are also [of all kinds] and difficult to understand clearly. The ones we usually come into contact with are [Cantonese], [Ningbo people], [Jiangbei people], [Shandong people], and [Pudong people]. After the September 18th Incident, we also saw many [Manchus] who had entered the Pass. Those who speak a few words of Beijing dialect claim to be [Beijing people], but they speak in a way that [Shanghai people] cannot understand and insist on acting like [Shanghai people].

This is how it is horizontally. Vertically, it is also a [grand spectacle].

Even among [Shanghai people], there is a distinction between [upper-class people] and [lower-class people]. Above the [upper-class people], there are even [great men]. Below the [lower-class people], there are even [minimum people]. Between the [upper-class people] and the [lower-class people], there are also [middle-class people] who are neither upper nor lower. Besides the upper, middle, and lower classes, there is also a type of [loafer] that cannot be classified.

In addition to the upper, middle, and lower classes, [people] are further divided into [lucky people], [blessed people], [scholars], [famous people], [important people], [poor people], [suffering people], [troublemakers], [awkward people], [capable people], [useless people], [fashionable people], [unlucky people], etc., too many to count or describe. Even more strangely, those who grow up on the same land are divided into [city people] and [country people].

[People] are so complicated that they cannot avoid [competing and robbing] and [deceiving each other]. The ideals of [great harmony] and [equality] are only good for deceiving the biggest fools in the world!

Subletter 189

— Hualing

[Subletters] in Shanghai are truly arrogant. Subtenants fear them like tigers, and even landlords must be cautious in their presence.

Subletters habitually owe landlords rent for two or three months, which is considered polite. However, if subtenants owe subletters rent for ten or fifteen days, they will be met with disdain. A mere [cold shoulder] is not enough; usually, they will be [ordered to move out].

When war broke out in the Chinese area, the concessions also reduced rent for three months. The landlord suffered in silence, while the subletter grinned from ear to ear. Because a three-story building on a kiosk cost twenty yuan, and the top floor cost eighteen yuan, as soon as the rental notice was pasted, the rooms were rented out to refugees before the glue was dry. If subtenants dared to ask for a rent reduction, the subletter would snort and say, "It's already polite not to raise the rent."

The landlord pays for the water bill, so in addition to mopping the floor every day, the subletter must also turn on the tap every night and let it run until dawn, so as not to waste it and give the landlord a freebie. However, for the subtenant's electricity, the subletter implements [blackout drills] as soon as the first strike of twelve o'clock is heard on the Customs bell and locks the [main door]. If the subtenant replaces a 25-candlepower light bulb with a 32-candlepower one, the subletter will immediately come to the door to scold them.

The subletter occupies the public alley for cooking and washing clothes because they rent out the kitchen, claiming to be taking advantage of the landlord. However, if a subtenant who has nothing to do with it puts a footstool in the living room, the subletter will rush to it like chickens fighting for food, accompanied by a group of patching-up workers in cloth short jackets. The seats in second-class trams are not small, but because they are three coppers cheaper, they are packed so tightly that no water can leak through. The ticket seller has to display Zhao Zilong's skills in saving A Dou before Changban Slope in order to cut a bloody path to sell a few tickets. A friend wearing a Hangfang long gown and a Columbia hat is also squeezed into the crowd of sweating and stinking people. On the surface, he is undoubtedly a crane among chickens.

What about the first-class tram? Two disheveled, bare-legged modern misses, a middle-aged woman weighing seventy pounds, and five or six bright-faced, lively-looking middle-class Chinese (Note: Upper-class Chinese ride cars) are sitting there. The lazy people can stretch their legs and fall asleep on the seats. The door in the middle of the tram is like a chasm, clearly dividing the two classes of rich and poor, or rather, the distinction between the proletariat and the middle class. How unfair is this! However, the first-class trains and the officer's cabins of ships often feel frighteningly quiet. At the same time, in the fourth-class trains and the bottom cabins, there is often no place to stand. Running into four or five-story 洋房, sometimes, you can't find half a person in a big circle, but a pigeon-cage-like old house has to accommodate five or six households. "Behind vermilion gates, meat and wine are rancid; on the road lie frozen corpses." The unequal facts of humanity are almost everywhere. Is it only true of trams?

In the past, the trams that passed through Manwete Falong Village from Washington City, USA, and reached the left bank of the Botamai River (George Washington's hometown) separated the seats of white and black people, and the boundaries were extremely strict and could not be crossed. The unfortunate black people became the insulted in an unequal society. Our first and second-class tram seats can be freely taken with money, without any restrictions, and with one kick you are kicked out the door.

The landlord's position is like the position of the first wife. The subletter is like the position of the fierce and shrewish concubine. At the beginning of the year, naturally the concubine has the upper hand. As for the subtenant, it can be said that they are pitiful, being like the master under the concubine's tyranny, as long or as short as she wants. Sometimes the concubine is scolded by the first wife, and naturally it is the master's bad luck.

In Shanghai, subtenants have never been seen who don't stick out their tongues in front of the subletter. What's more, the subletter who has just risen from a subtenant is like 淌白 leaping to become a concubine, and can do anything.

Subtenants will not be able to sleep soundly until the subletters are overthrown.

Thoughts from the Tram 190

— Fu Yizhi

The tram on Route 3, "Ding Dong, Ding Dong," is approaching the stop at the intersection of Xinjiao Street. As soon as the iron gate opened, several friends jumped down whom I didn't consciously identify. Compared to black people, isn't it even better? An ancient poem says: "Others ride horses, I ride a donkey, carefully considering it, it's not as good; suddenly looking back at the porter, it's not enough to be better, but it's more than enough to be worse." Friends! May you comfort yourself with this and be patient!

The Four Company Commanders of the Northeast 192

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Ten

Abandoning His Post for a Soulmate, the Beauty Silently Approves

Inheriting the Family Fortune, the Young Hero Celebrates Joyously

Guan Yaowu held a cigarette in his mouth, listening quietly. When he heard this, he could no longer contain himself. He pressed his hand on the corner of the table, straightening his body, as if about to stand up and speak. Madam Jiang waved her hand and said: "No need to say it, I understand your meaning completely. To tell you the truth, I received the news last night that Commander Zhao is willing to resign his command for this marriage. Don't look down on our girl; she has a mind of her own. She said, 'This is not right; no one should lose their future for the sake of marriage. No girl wants to bear that guilt.' Just Commander Zhao saying this is enough to make people happy. Besides, we didn't have enough to celebrate the New Year last year, and we had to pawn our cotton coats. Thanks to him, he helped us get them back from the pawnshop counter. Now I understand; he pawned his fur coat for the money." Guan Yaowu said: "Strange! How do you know all these things?" Madam Jiang smiled and said: "Don't ask how I know. Are the things I said correct or not?" Guan Yaowu said: "Absolutely right. How can you know so clearly?" Madam Jiang smiled: "I can't tell you the source of my information; if I did, I wouldn't be able to get any more news in the future." Guan Yaowu laughed: "So you plan to keep getting news. Does this mean you approve of this marriage?" Madam Jiang said: "To be honest, I have nothing to say against someone like Commander Zhao. I'm just thinking that soldiers only have public affairs and no private affairs. If my child marries out, she'll still be living like a single woman, so why should I want her to marry out? Because of this, I haven't been able to decide. Now I hear that he also feels that our concerns are valid and is willing to give up being a commander. Not only our girl feels deeply grateful, but I also feel unworthy (158)."

The Key to the Modern Woman's Make-up (Part 2) 193

— Bingyu

Because the shape of the lips varies, some thick and some thin, and the structure of the mouth also varies, some large and some small, such as trumpet mouths and carp mouths, there are thousands of differences in size and width. Moreover, the lips and mouth are closely related, and the color of the lips also varies. If artificial means are not used to remedy them, it will affect the beauty of the eyebrows, eyes, nose, and other parts. Now I will talk about the method of applying lipstick: Generally speaking, the color of the lips is different for each person, with some being dark black, pale white, or grayish-red. These lip colors are very unsightly in appearance and cannot attract the enthusiasm of others, so it is necessary to transform the color of the lips. The transformation procedure depends on the size of the mouth and the thickness of the lips. If the person has thick lips and a large mouth, half of the outer side of the lips can be painted with a very light red, and the inner side of the lips should be painted with a dark red. Then, people with large mouths will appear to have small mouths. If the person has a small mouth and thin lips, then both the inner and outer sides of the lips should be painted with a uniformly bright red color, which can naturally make them appear thicker and larger. However, it should not be painted too wide and should be carefully considered. If it is a trumpet mouth, then the upper half of the upper lip and the lower half of the lower lip can be left unpainted, while the lower half of the upper lip and the upper half of the lower lip should be painted with dark red to correct the mouth's shortcomings. Therefore, when applying makeup, never forget the individuality of the lips. Speaking of lip rouge, there is a non-fading red rose-colored rouge. This rouge was originally manufactured by American Dr. Young as a disinfectant for surgical operations and was named Mercury Chromium. At that time, it was only a substitute for iodine. Later, after several trials, even when exposed to water, it would not fade for three or four days. Now, it has become even more advanced, not only with beautiful colors but also with the effects of disinfection and preservation, so it can better exert its appeal when kissing a lover. The above is the key to applying lipstick. Please pay special attention to ladies and modern misses.

The Key to Dyeing Fingernails

The method of dyeing fingernails is very simple, but there are many points that cannot be ignored. The currently popular fingernail styles are roughly the plow-shaped Shade and the iron stone-shaped Diamond, both with sharp angles. After applying peach-colored enamel nail polish, it will produce a beautiful luster. However, when decorating fingernails, you should first consider whether your hands are suitable for decoration. In other words, you should see if your finger shape has the qualification for decoration. Why? Because many people's hands have rough and dark skin, wide and flat finger shapes, and short and thick fingers. No matter how decorated, these hands cannot evoke a sense of beauty. They should possess the elements of "jade-like slender fingers" and "tender as bamboo shoots" to be worthy of decoration. I often see women's hands with dirt accumulated in their fingernails and their fingertips blackened by smoke, while their fingernails are dyed peach red. This is truly contradictory. Therefore, ladies, please first solve the problem of cleanliness from the root before talking about decoration. As for dyeing, there is one point that we should pay special attention to because many viruses often start from manicures, which is a type of whitlow bacteria in medicine. Some even cause the finger joints to become whitlow and numb, and others cause pyogenic sputum due to the invasion of mold from the fingernails. Therefore, when trimming fingernails, they should be disinfected. The current common disinfection method is to first wash away the dirt with lukewarm soapy water, then soak them in a thousand times diluted mercury solution for five minutes, wipe the fingertips dry, and then soak them in a 70% alcohol solution to gradually peel off the epidermis on the fingernails. Finally, apply peach-colored enamel nail polish, so that there will be no dangerous viruses.
